10a1(1): gnas pa yi// khang pa mthon po rnams dang 'bigs byed ri rtse 'gron pa'i bal glang dang // gdugs dang rnga ya ba bud med g.yog 'khor rin chen
10a2(1): gser dang rta rnams dang // bzang mdzes de dag kun kyang sngon gyi sbyin pa'i dge ba'i rnam smin yin// ban du ka ltar rtsa dmar dgun chang gser snod bzang por legs
10a3(1): blugs pa// yongs dag a mra'i smin ltar dri zhim ud pa la 'gying zhing ldem// na chung zhen pa mna' sgog dus kyis stobs shing yams grangs mang 'grim pa// mchog tu dge
10a4(1): ba de rgyu srin pa yin zhes blo gros dag pas gsungs// gser gyi bag skas rkeng bcings snyan smras 'dzum zhing smin ma ya cig spyod// mig yangs rnag thug dkar nag
10a5(1): 'byes la sgra 'ab ba me tog phreng bkris pa'i// na chung bzang mo brlar rgyas nyid legs byas rnams kyi bran ltar byed cing // tshogs bsags 'bras de sbyin pa'i che ba nyid
10a6(1): ces zas gtsang sras pos gsungs// de lta lags pas bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag thugs chud pa// shin tu rgyus pa'i chu ltar gyur pa snying po dri ma med
10a7(1): ba dang // lha'i skye bo dang gru'i gnas su gyur pa// tshul khrims 'dren pa ma yin zhing rgya che ba'i chu dang ldan pa dge ba la rnam par rtog pa'i zla ba shar ba'i dbang gis// ting
10a8(1): nge 'dzin sna tshogs rgyas pa'i dus kyi rlabs kyis byang chub kyi yan lag skyon med pa'i nor bu mang po kun tu g.yangs pa// sems kyi 'og gni la 'phags pa'i lam yang
10b1(1): lag brgyad pa'i thonan po bden pa/ 'bras bu'i bye zag zab pa/ gang zag chen pa'i mu snan chub/ 'phags pa'i bden pa dang / yang dag par snang ba dang / 
10b2(1): 'phrul gyi rkang pa'i shing ljon pas mdzes par byas pa/ dran pa nye bar bzhag pa'i ngogs dang ldan pa/ sgrib pa'i ro mi gnas pa/ sbyangs pa'i yon tan goms pa'i dag pa
10b3(1): mu tig gi 'a byis kyi khog lus dang ldan pa/ mngon par rtogs pa'i chos nyid gnyid mi dpogs shing za ba pa/ rgyun mi 'chad par klog pa dang / kha ton byed pa'i sku rgya che
10b4(1): 'byung ba/ 'phags pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun gyi rgya mtsho chen po la bdag gsol ba 'tshal lo// 'di lta sti srid pa'i 'gro ba gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa du ma nas
10b5(1): dge ba'i sa bon btab pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa/ gzhal med khang gis bani gcig par gyur pa/ bzod pa dang / nges pa dang / byams pa dang / chu
10b6(1): khrims dang / thos pa dang / zhi ba'i gnas/ bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung don gyi de kho na ma lus par rtogs pa/ yongs su shes pas bsgoms pas dran pa nye bar
10b7(1): gnas pa/ yang dag pa'i ye shes mthong bas log par lta ba'i ra ba rI ba bsal ba/ legs par brjod cing shis la rgya che ba'i mi dang ldan pa'i skye bo bla ma la bsnyen
10b8(1): bkur byed pa dang / mngon du smra ba dang / phyag 'tshal ba la sogs pa'i tshul bzang po dang ldan zhing mdong gsol che bas spen pa rnams bskyed pa/ ston gyi zla ba nya ba'i
11a1(1): 'od zer dag pa lta bu'i yid 'byung ba/ sbyin bdag chen po che ba'i bdag nyid can ming 'di zhes bya ba 'di ni/ khyim bdag legs sbyin dang

11b1(1): pa'in/ skyabs su bos pa'i chos ston pa/ 'gro ba la dge ba'i bya dka' ba'i phrin las rnams kyis/ chos thams cad thugs su chud pas rnam par sangs rgyas rnam

11b3(1): gi nor bu chen pos nabs kyi sor mo kun tu bskor ba/ gser gyi mchog sdang ltar gsal ba/ sbru la rdo rje dang lcags kyu dang / pad+ma dang / nya dang / rgyu la mtshan dang / 
11b4(1): gdugs dang / 'khor lo la sogs pa'i mtshan rnams kyi mtshan mnga' ba/ pad+ma'i 'byung gnas rnams la/ snad mdzad kyi 'od kyi phreng ba bye brag med par khya pa
11b5(1): rgyas par 'gengs pa/ bung ba'i tshogs ltar sde ba'i gtsug tor gyi nang nas kun 'byung ba'i 'od kyi dra bas phyogs kyi dkyil 'khor ma lus par bkra bar byas pas
11b6(1): kha na ma tho ba med par zhugs pa/ 'phags pa'i bden pa ston pa/ zhi bar gzhol ba'i lam du 'dren pa/ 'jig rten sgrol ba mnyes gshin pa// gnyen gcig pu
11b7(1): mu stegs can ngan pa'i rgol ba rnams kyis gsung dang / thugs dang / dpa' ba dang / mthu la mi gnod pa gtsang ma'i sras yul rnams kun la sred pa 'byung ba rgyun
11b8(1): skams byed pa'i rgyu/ skye bo mkhas pa rnams ni sad par bya phyir shar gyur pa/ bag la nyal gyi ra ba ri ba bsal ba ye shes snang ba'i mchog/ sa rnams mtha' dag
12a1(1): snang ba phyogs rnams thams cad snang mdzad pa// phyag dang nabs dang dbu ni rab tu byin zhing tshul khrims dang // smon lam dag gis byang chub lam bzang
12a2(1): yang dag bsgrubs gyur pa// srid pa'i 'gro ba'i dug gis snye ma'i steng du lhung ba yi// skye dgu rnams la kha na mtho med pa ston mdzad pa// srid pa rnam pa gsum du 'jig pa
12a3(1): bcom ldan 'das stobs bcu'i stobs dang ldan pa/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi mnga' ba/ dpa' ba dang / mthu khan ma mtho ba med pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos brgyan

12a5(1): bathugs su chud pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i 'phags pa nyan thos kyi dge 'dun rab tu zhi ba dang / tshul khrims dang / thos pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / bzod pa dang / byams pa
12a6(1): sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa/ nyon mongs pa'i ra ba ri ba dang / ling tog ma lus par bsal ba/ 'khor ba'i rang bzhin rig pa dang / phyogs phyogs kyi gtsug lag khang dang /

12a8(1): dum la phan gdags par spel bar mdzad pa/ yang dag pa'i dran pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / dga'i bathob pa las mnyams pa/ phung po lnga spyir skad cig par yang dag par
12b1(1): so sor rtogs pa'i yid la byed ba skyed pa'i mdo sde dang / 'dul ba dang / chos mngon pa dang / skyes pa'i rabs dang / gleng gzhi dang / tshigs su bcang ba dang / rtags pa
12b2(1): brjod pa dang / de lta bu byung ba dang / gtan pab pa'i gtam gyi sems spangs pa/ rang gi lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyi 'jug pa dran pa nye bar gnas pa rgyu ba dbang po dang
12b3(1): stobs dang / byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bden pa dang / 'phags pa'i lam dang / dran pa nye bar bzhag pa sgom pa goms pas dad pa thob pa/ bum thugs kyis nyams
12b4(1): dga' la// re sul mthon po dpag bsam nags mang dang // ri bag pa rnams ni gang dag bzhugs pa dang // shing gi me tog 'phrul bas dri zhim byas pa'i ser bu dang

13a8(1): yod pa'i daphyis kha bye ba'i theg mas rnam par sbas pa/ nye bar 'dul ba dang ldan la/ nor bu mchog rdal grub pa'i chung ma'i skye bo gnas shing bya'i khru dga' se sgra 'byin pas
